It has now been decided to first conduct a city (Shanghai) flight tomorrow (i.e. today), and the long-distance flight is scheduled for this Friday and Saturday, and will depart when the weather is good. The landing points are Nantong, Zhenjiang, Nanjing, Wuhu, Anqing, Jiujiang, Hankou, Yuezhou, Changsha, Shashi, and Yichang, then return to Shanghai. After a few days of rest, fly to Ningbo, Wenzhou, Xiamen, and Fuzhou. The Jiangfeng aircraft will be left at the Mawei Aviation Office as a training aircraft, and I will return to Shanghai by boat. Currently, one aircraft manufactured by this plant will be completed by the end of the year and will be deployed on the Ninghai ship. As for the Jiangfeng aircraft for long-distance flight, it was manufactured in 1931. The engine is American Rott type, with a horsepower of 1654, a fully loaded weight of 1116 kg, a firing speed of 190 kilometers, a cruising speed of 157 kilometers, a landing speed of 91 kilometers, a sea level ascent of 136 meters, and a peak altitude of 3810 meters. The type of seaplane is for reconnaissance training, etc.

According to the Guo Wen News Agency, Mr. Zeng Yijing is an expert in self-made aircraft in China. With low funds and simple factories, based on his knowledge and great perseverance, he finally created many military aircraft such as Jiangfeng and Jianghe. He will conduct a test flight in seven provinces tomorrow, and in the future, aviation to save the country will not depend on others. His work is very great. Mr. Zeng has an article "The Success of Self-Made Aircraft in Our Country", published in the first issue of the Far East Monthly. If you want to read the first self-made aircraft in our country, you can attach a stamp of one corner and send a letter to the newspaper office at No. 221 Saipo Road to read it.

Painful Words of Northeastern Returnees

Japan Wants to Destroy My Northeast Nationalities with the Old Tricks of Destroying Korea

Yesterday, a reporter from the National Communication Agency met with Mr. Zhang Zhichen, a teacher at a primary school in Changchun, who fled from the Northeast. He told us in detail the recent situation of the puppet organization and the various sinister plots of the Japanese to rule the Northeast. The details are recorded below.

Completion of the Duntou Railway

The Duntou Railway (from Dunhua to Tumen River), which is a section of the former Jihui Railway, has been under active construction by the Japanese since mid-May last year under the entrustment of the South Manchurian Railway Company. It was fully completed and announced on April 20 this year and has begun commercial operations. The entire line is 192 kilometers long, starting from Dunhua and passing through 15 stations: Daqiao, Dashitou, Haberling, Nangou, Liangbingtai, Mingyuegou, Chatiaogou, Yushuchuan, Laotou Gou, Tongfosi, Chaoyangchuan, Yanji, Mopanshan, Weizigou, Nanyang, and reaching Tumen River. In the future, the Japanese army in Korea can directly reach North Manchuria by this railway. Before this railway was completed, the Japanese army in Korea had to transfer via Dalian to reach North Manchuria. Now, they can directly reach North Manchuria from Duntou and Dunji, which is much faster than in the past. Moreover, the counties along the Duntou Railway are the richest in production in the Northeast. The annual output of goods is over 4,210,297,511,407 shi, the area is 45,440 square miles, and the population is 700,7370 people. Now, they have all fallen into the hands of the Japanese, and it is truly heartbreaking to say that recovery is out of the question.

Two Planned Roads

After the completion of the Duntou Railway, the Japanese plan to build the Laha Railway (from Lafa to Harbin) and the Yanhai Railway (from Yanji to Hailin) to rule my entire Northeast and develop various rich resources. This plan has already begun to prepare and a large number of engineers have been sent to inspect and measure along the two lines. Construction is expected to begin in August and September of this year.

Tax Revenue Drops Sharply Compared to Before

Since the puppet organization was declared established under the wing of the Japanese, all administrative powers have been controlled by the Japanese. The puppet Puyi has no right to interfere. In order to settle unemployed Japanese in the Northeast, the Japanese have tried their best to increase the number of institutions, and some organizations have as many as twenty or more departments, with up to 600 employees. Therefore, expenditures have increased sharply, and the import of Japanese goods into the territory of the puppet organization is also exempt from tariffs, resulting in a sharp drop in tax revenue. Compared to before the September 18th Incident, it is short by six-tenths. In order to balance the budget, the Japanese authorities levy various exorbitant taxes on Chinese operating in the interior and vigorously enforce the public sale of opium to increase their income. Currently, opium dens are everywhere in the territory of the puppet organization, and each opium pipe is taxed one yuan in Manchu currency per day, which is euphemistically called entertainment donation. Other places such as gambling dens and brothels are even more numerous. In short, the Northeastern compatriots have become the fish on the Japanese knife.

Volunteer Army Rises Up on the Occasion

However, there is one thing that is enough to comfort me, that is, the volunteer army in various places is becoming more and more active because the green gauze account has started. Currently, the Kwantung Army of the Japanese army has formulated a plan to encircle and suppress this volunteer army, hoping to eliminate the confidant's trouble as soon as possible. The volunteer army is unpredictable and its whereabouts are uncertain, and there are also no lack of patriotic people in the puppet army who are waiting for an opportunity to revolt, so the Japanese tricks have been detected by the volunteer army and they can calmly deal with them. The strategy adopted by the current volunteer army is guerrilla warfare, adhering to the twelve-character secret of "you come, I go," "avoid the important and take the light," and "take advantage of the situation," so that the Japanese army cannot carry out a large-scale encirclement. In addition, bandits are everywhere, looting is heard, which makes the Japanese side even more overwhelmed and struggling to deal with it.

Implementing a Policy of Eradicating the Race Through Writing

As for the schools in the territory of the puppet organization, the teachers are all Japanese. The curriculum is required to have Japanese as a compulsory subject, which takes up hours every day. English and American languages each take up one hour, and the remaining one hour is half an hour for exercise and half an hour for Chinese. The Japanese desire to destroy the race by destroying the Korean race through writing can be seen here. Moreover, students in the same school, Chinese children must stand at attention and salute when they see Japanese children on the way, otherwise they will be insulted. It is expected that in fifteen years, millions of people in the Northeast will become cattle and horses of the Japanese.

Chinese Farmers Waiting to Die

Finally, Mr. Zhang also said that millions of Chinese farmers in various parts of the Northeast are now waiting to die. After the Japanese occupied the Northeast by force, in order to implement their immigration policy, they successively transported unemployed people from various parts of the country to Korea to reclaim wasteland, and then moved Korean farmers to the Northeast empty-handed to reclaim wasteland. Unexpectedly, these Korean farmers had long forgotten the pain of their own country's demise and recognized the thief as their father, arbitrarily seizing the homes of Chinese farmers, snatching cultivated land and agricultural tools as their own. If the Chinese farmers resisted, they were brutally killed, and even forced the Chinese farmers to be their slaves for driving. As for rape and plunder, they are still being spared. Alas, what crime have the farmers in the Northeast committed to be the slaves of slaves in a conquered country? I deeply hope that our government authorities and the people of the whole country will rise up together to save the Northeastern compatriots who have no way to go to heaven and no way to enter the earth, and to preserve a portion of vitality for the country.

Yangtze River Flooding

Affects Upstream Commercial Goods

Shayi Hakka Gang Has Telegraphed Shanghai to Reduce Shipping

The Han River was flooded in 2020, reaching 42 feet and 6 inches, which had already flooded the city and turned it into a vast ocean, causing a rare disaster. Last year, the National Government's Flood Relief Committee used American wheat to provide work for relief and built river dikes as a fundamental plan to prevent floods. However, the river water has risen again this year. As of yesterday, the water level in Hankou, according to the telegram, has reached 39 feet and 4 inches, which is only 2 feet and 78 inches lower than the highest water level in the past year. The water is level with the shore in the lower reaches of the river. If the water rises further, it will inevitably enter the city from the ditches, and the newly built dike gate will also be blocked if necessary to prevent danger. Yangtze River ships traveling up and down the river between Jiujiang and Hankou have been banned from express trains. Patrol Jiangsi has added red warning lights to dangerous places along the river to avoid accidents on merchant ships. According to the telegram from Yichang, the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, the water level continues to increase, exceeding 32 feet. There is no embankment there. If the water increases sharply, there is a danger of flooding the city. Recently, a large number of spun yarn in Shanghai is being shipped to Yichang and Shashi. Due to the impact of the flood, Shayi Hakka Gang has telegraphed to Shanghai, ordering that the spun yarn should not be shipped in full, and only a small part should be loaded first to avoid the flood.

First Batch

Argentine Wheat Imports

The First Three Ships Carry 25,000 Tons

A Breakthrough in South American Trade

Agricultural production is overstocked in various countries, and they are suffering from a lack of sales channels. However, the flour mills in our country are greedy for its cheap price and have successively ordered the first batch of American wheat and then Australian wheat. Now they have placed orders to South America, and a batch has been shipped. It is the first time that South American wheat has been shipped to China. The details are reported as follows.

Purchase Quantity

After purchasing huge amounts of American and Australian wheat, the major flour mills in Shanghai, such as Fuxin and Maoxin, have also tried to purchase a batch of wheat from South America this year to be shipped to China for comparison. However, because South American wheat has never been sold to the Far East, and there is no precedent for how much flour it produces, the first time they temporarily ordered 60,000 tons of Argentine wheat from foreign merchants on a trial basis to be delivered to Shanghai. The contract was signed long ago.

Ferry Transport

The 60,000 tons of South American wheat, after Shuangwen's plans, are to be transported to Shanghai by eight ferries. Some of it may need to be shipped to Hankou for delivery. The wheat is already being shipped, with three ships carrying a total of 25,000 tons to Shanghai first. The remaining cargo will be carried by five more ships. The first batch of wheat is managed by Geddes & Co. and De Foe & Co. LkuisDreefuaCo... etc.

Released After Inquiry at the Police Station

Guomin News Agency reports that a company of soldiers, about one hundred, from the 166th Brigade of the 56th Division under Liu Heding, were en route from Yingzhou, Anhui, to Fujian. Japanese Merchants Refuse to Use Indian Cotton

Textile Association Decided Yesterday

All Factories Have Been Notified Accordingly

Switching to Chinese Cotton or Temporarily Reducing Work

Datong News Agency reports that since the British government implemented a blockade of Japanese goods, triggering intense commercial warfare against Japan, it has provoked opposition throughout Japan. The Shanghai Japanese Textile Association received a telegram from the Osaka headquarters the day before yesterday, announcing that from now on, all Japanese yarn factories in Shanghai should refuse to use Indian cotton to retaliate. The Japanese Textile Association convened an emergency meeting yesterday afternoon at 5 PM to discuss measures. Details are as follows:

Telegram from Osaka Headquarters

Since the outbreak of the Anglo-Japanese trade war, the Osaka Japanese Textile Industry Federation immediately telegraphed the Shanghai Japanese Textile Association, instructing all factories to unanimously refuse to use Indian cotton to show support, and also to boycott all other British goods. The translated telegram is as follows: (omitted above) Britain has inexplicably imposed a blockade on our (Japanese self-designation) trade, causing significant losses to our countrymen. The situation is now even more serious. Most of the businesses and factories of our countrymen in Britain have been forced to shut down and quietly return home. Although our countrymen wish to be magnanimous, because it is related to the rise and fall of the national fortune, we must regard it as a particularly serious matter. Our textile industry should especially refuse to use Indian cotton to show retaliation and should earnestly advise overseas Chinese to boycott and not use other British goods until Britain achieves the goal of opening up free trade. We hereby inform your association and hope you will proceed promptly. (omitted below)

Yesterday Evening's Emergency Meeting

The Shanghai Japanese Textile Association, after receiving the telegram from the Osaka headquarters, immediately convened an emergency meeting at its headquarters yesterday afternoon at 5 PM, gathering more than thirty representatives from Japanese yarn factories in Shanghai. As a result of the meeting, they unanimously insisted on complying with the telegram from the Osaka headquarters. From now on, all will refuse to use Indian cotton and will temporarily use Chinese cotton as a substitute for the unified textile raw materials (i.e., cotton). If Chinese cotton is lacking, they will implement a reduction in work to show their determination. At the same time, the Japanese Residents Association notified all Japanese residents in Shanghai that they will also strictly boycott all kinds of British goods. The meeting lasted until after 7 PM.

Textile Association Announcement

At the emergency meeting of Japanese yarn factory representatives yesterday, a draft announcement was also prepared on the spot, printed overnight, and scheduled to be distributed to all Japanese yarn factories in Shanghai this morning for unified compliance. The full text of the announcement is as follows: Regarding the matter of urgent announcement, the British government has recently suddenly implemented a fierce trade war against us and blockaded our trade organizations in England. Our association received a telegram from the Osaka headquarters, instructing to immediately instruct all overseas Chinese merchants and yarn factories in Shanghai to uniformly refuse to use Indian cotton from now on to show retaliation. Our association convened a representative conference yesterday to discuss measures and decided to take a resolute attitude and strong spirit, absolutely comply with the Osaka headquarters' telegram, completely refuse to purchase and use Indian cotton, and temporarily substitute it with Chinese cotton. If Chinese cotton is lacking, Indian cotton must not be purchased privately, cutting off the path of patriotism. They should immediately reduce work with pain to show their determination. We hope that all factories will comply with it as a whole. This is a special announcement.

Will Inspect New Coins According to Regulations

Second General Meeting of New Coin Audit Committee

Resolved: The Standing Committee will submit the new coins to inspection organizations both in Shanghai and other ports for inspection. Other ports include Tianjin and Beiping. China

Cotton Production Improvement Association Annual Meeting: Preliminary Hearing

Important Discussion on the Decline of Domestic Cotton

The cotton shortage in this city has aroused deep social concern. Although the government has established a large Sino-American 50 million cotton and wheat loan, our country, founded on agriculture, has a cotton production that cannot meet the demand, which is a fundamental problem. The construction bureaus of various provinces are now doing their best to improve it. The Cotton Production Improvement Association is scheduled to convene a meeting to discuss it. Details are as follows:

Decrease in Domestic Cotton

The cotton-producing regions of our country, such as Jiangsu, Henan, Shandong, Shanxi, Hebei, Shaanxi, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, and Liaoning, had a national cotton production of 10,220,779 dan in 1918. And Shaanxi, Zhejiang, Hunan, and Liaoning were not included. In 1931, the national cotton production was 6,399,780 dan, a difference of more than one-third. The reasons for the decrease are roughly the unstable political situation, years of drought and flood, dumping of foreign cotton, reduced purchasing power, and the resulting rural decline.

Establishment of Test Fields

The government, in order to promote and improve cotton planting, established the first cotton cultivation test field in Zhengding in 1915, the second cotton cultivation test field in Tongzhou, and the third cotton cultivation test field in Wuchang. The fourth cotton cultivation test field was established in Beijing in 1918. The Central Government established a model cotton planting field directly under its administration in Zhangde in 1916. Later, due to financial difficulties, they were successively closed. Only the test field in Zhengding was changed to the National Cotton Cultivation Test Field by the Ministry of Industry. Now, the provincial governments are actively promoting it. For example, the construction bureaus of Zhejiang, Hunan, and Shaanxi have all established cotton cultivation test fields. Hubei established a cotton industry improvement committee by cotton merchants.

Cotton Production Meeting

Since the establishment of the China Cotton Production Improvement Association, it has presented to the Ministry of Industry, seeing that our country's cotton production is backward and the raw materials for clothing cannot be self-sufficient, resulting in huge imports of foreign cotton, foreign yarn, and foreign cloth. 1. Establishing a national cotton cultivation test product. 2. Reorganizing the provincial cotton cultivation test fields in various provinces. 3. Setting up cotton seed fields in suitable cotton-growing counties. The second annual meeting will be held in Shanghai on July 9th and 10th, and important cases such as improving domestic cotton will be put forward for discussion at that time.

Improvement Plan

Yesterday, a cotton industry expert told a Xinsheng News Agency reporter that it is extremely appropriate to help and improve our country's cotton industry after its decline. 1. Fundamental Solution: Protecting domestic cotton and restricting the import of foreign cotton; systematically organizing the improvement of the cotton industry. 2. Short-term Solution: Cooperation between producers and consumers; promoting domestic cotton and adopting domestic cotton. Moreover, countries that produce cotton all restrict the import of foreign cotton. For example, the United States prohibits the import of all cotton plants and their products, including the entire plant and unprocessed flower clothes seeds, all waste flowers, and cotton used for packaging. It is not allowed to be imported, ostensibly to prevent the boll weevil, but in reality, it fears the invasion of foreign cotton.

To Stop Hankou City from Levying Taxes on Goods

The Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association received a letter from the Hankou Silk and Satin Trade Association, stating that the Hankou business tax collection agency suddenly went to various shops to inspect goods. For the silk and satin industry operating in the business of silk, ramie, and ge cloth, they were regarded as foreign goods and could not be taxed at the same rate as domestic silk and satin. And to stop the excessive demands exceeding the provisions of the outline regulations stipulated by the Ministry, so as to comply with the tax law and ensure business stability.

The Shanghai Haining Foreign Firm, founded by American merchants, has its manufacturing plant located west of Xiangyan Bridge, covering an area of more than thirty acres. Taxi Hits Pedestrian

At the corner of Avenue Edward VII and Rue Cardinal Mercier at approximately 8:50 PM last night, a pedestrian, Mr. Jia, approximately thirty years old, wearing a white cloth short shirt, black silk pants, and white canvas shoes, was about to board a tram at the tram stop when a Yunfei taxi, registered as 12254, came speeding from east to west. Mr. Jia tried to avoid it, but was knocked to the ground and his head was crushed. He lost consciousness. Seizing Family Property, a Big Disturbance in the Ancestral Hall

US Consulate Personally Investigates

Ms. Shen Cai, a local woman, is 67 years old. She had only one daughter, named Dan Ying, who married Mike Caven (transliteration), an American engineer, and had two daughters, Bao Juan, 16, and Xiu Juan, 15, who are currently studying at Qiming Girls' School. However, Dan Ying passed away in the fourth year of the Republic of China (1915). Mike then married Ms. Chen of Xin Longhua as his second wife, and they now have five children. Because Ms. Cai is old and has no one to rely on, she lives with her goddaughter, Ms. Chen, and her son-in-law, Mike Caven, at No. 22 Chen Family Residence, Tushanwan, West Shanghai, where they have lived for over 20 years. Unexpectedly, Ms. Shen Cai passed away due to illness at around 11:00 AM on the 10th of this month. Her son-in-law, Mike Caven, who is currently in Changzhou building a hydroelectric plant, was immediately telegraphed to return. Upon hearing the news, Mike rushed back to the Chen Family Residence overnight to handle the funeral arrangements. In accordance with Chinese customs and etiquette, he respectfully mourned and provided a dignified burial, showing great filial piety. However, Shen Xiangdi, the nephew of Ms. Shen Cai (a 35-year-old steelworker), gathered a group of people yesterday morning and caused a great disturbance at the mourning hall, forbidding the burial and vehemently demanding inheritance of his aunt's estate from Mike Caven, behaving unreasonably. Unable to bear the harassment, Mike reported the matter to the US consulate. Upon receiving the report, Mr. Meterkert (transliteration), the US consul stationed in Shanghai, visited the Chen Family Residence in the countryside at 11:00 AM yesterday with an interpreter to investigate. He then returned to the Second Branch Office of the Sixth District in Xujiahui to request police protection. After receiving the report, Director Wu immediately dispatched police officers to suppress the disturbance. Shen Xiangdi still dared to unreasonably obstruct Mike Caven, and the police took Shen to the station for temporary detention until the coffin was finally sealed at 5:00 PM.

A Patrol Officer Dies in the Line of Duty

The Solemn Funeral Ceremony Yesterday

The case of He Jianqing, the Director of the Pharmacy Department of the Chinese Red Cross General Hospital on Haig Road, a professor of pharmacology at Shanghai Medical College, and a native of Changzhou, who was assassinated at noon on the 3rd of last month in front of No. 297 Haig Road while returning home for lunch, was previously reported. At the time, Gu Zhihui, a Chinese patrol officer No. 127 from the French Concession's Shanzhong Road Police Station, was patrolling east of Maqi Road on Haig Road and was shot in the hip by thugs before He, causing him to fall. Document Typing Service with Chinese Typewriter

The Chinese typewriter invented by Mr. Yu Binqi, patented by the National Government, has used all domestic materials since its improvement after the September 18th Incident (Mukden Incident). The machine is sturdy, sensitive, and requires little practice to type 30 characters per minute. Government agencies, companies, banks, lawyers, and accountants are all happy to purchase it. However, due to cost limitations, it cannot be universally adopted, which is deeply regrettable. Nevertheless, requests from all sectors continue to pour in. Now, for convenience, a document typing and printing service has been established, specializing in typing documents, official correspondence, and lectures at reasonable prices. Various typewriter fonts are available, all made of steel, resistant to wear, and capable of producing more than ten copies at a time with carbon paper. Using wax paper, hundreds of copies can be printed with a mimeograph machine. In the future, all sectors requiring these services can have them provided. Furthermore, to meet the social demand for typing personnel, a Chinese typewriter training school has been specially established to train typists and introduce them to jobs, also as a means of alleviating unemployment. The office is located at China Industrial Development Company on Sanma Road (Nanjing East Road), where visitors are welcome to view and test the equipment.

This City

The Defense Corps Will Be Reorganized

New Regulations Have Been Passed by the Municipal Government

Immediate Implementation of Examination of All Members

The Shanghai Defense Corps Management Committee will be reorganized and actively consolidated. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the Central News Agency visited Xie Shouquan, the staff member of the committee, who said the following:

Consolidating Corps Affairs

The Second National Internal Affairs Conference resolved to consolidate the defense corps in various regions to strengthen local defense. In accordance with these regulations, the committee plans to change the Shanghai Defense Corps Management Committee to the Shanghai Defense Association and has drafted regulations to be submitted to the Municipal Government for review. It has been approved by the Municipal Council and forwarded to the Municipal Assembly for review. It can be implemented once the general meeting has passed it.

Examining Members

The Shanghai Defense Corps has more than 5,000 members, but they have not been examined, which is not serious enough. In order to improve the corps' service capabilities, the committee decided at this session of the Standing Committee to implement examinations to emphasize assessment and selection. Therefore, it has distributed examination forms to the regimental commanders of various districts to select officers to conduct detailed inspections with the team leaders and ordered them to complete the work within ten days and submit it to the committee for review and decision on acceptance. After the examination is completed, if too many members are dismissed, new members will be recruited to replenish the original number.

Crackdown on Illegal Opium Sales

Over Twenty Tins of Indian Opium Seized

Song Bingzheng, a Chinese detective from the Industry Bureau's Narcotics Department, received a secret report the day before yesterday (the 11th) stating that someone was running an opium den on the upper floor of the Chunji Silk and Satin Store at No. 87 Guangdong Road and selling opium. After receiving the report, Detective Song immediately reported to Chief Inspector Lu Liankui, who, together with the Western Inspector, dispatched a large number of detectives led by Detective Song to arrest the suspects at 10:30 AM. They found several sets of smoking paraphernalia and three large copper pots for burning opium. They then searched the hidden area in the room and seized over twenty tins of Indian opium, estimated to be worth over ten thousand yuan. Detective Song and others, with the evidence in hand, immediately detained three men and one woman in the room and brought them, along with the opium, to the police station. Under interrogation, Feng Zihui, Zhang Zihua, Wu Binan, and Yang Xie were identified. They claimed that someone else was running the opium business. The police station ordered them to be temporarily detained pending a request to the court for trial.

Shanghai Ningbo Jiangsu Tobacco Industries

The Federation Established Simultaneously Yesterday

Send Joint Telegram to the Central Government Requesting No Change in Tobacco Tax Rate

The Shanghai Ningbo Jiangsu Tobacco Industry Federation and the Wine Industry Federation have completed preparations and received approval from the City Party Department. Yesterday, they held their inaugural meetings in the assembly hall of the City Chamber of Commerce. The details are as follows:

Tobacco Industry Federation

The inaugural meeting was held at 9:00 AM yesterday. Over fifty representatives from various counties in Jiangsu Province attended. The association's charter was then passed, and Chen Liangyu, Zhang Suhou, Yu Xunlu, Shen Weiting, Cao Gexian, Wang Zhaoru, Jiang Xiangqing, Qiu Zizhen, Yao Daisi, Wang Wenqing, Wang Songfen, Wang Chunshan, Zhang Songji, Zhu Boxuan, and Liu Dingxin were elected as the fifteen executive committee members. Xia Jifu, Chen Ruilin, Xu Xichun, Li Xiantao, Wang Zhisheng, Chen Shihao, and Liu Zhuren were elected as the seven supervisory committee members. Dai Zhuoan and Li Zisen were elected as the two alternate supervisors. The following resolutions were then passed: 1. Improve the tobacco and alcohol license regulations. 2. Absolutely refuse the bidding system and oppose non-industry personnel from handling tobacco and alcohol tax matters. 3. Before the new tobacco and alcohol tax regulations are promulgated, send a telegram to the Ministry of Finance requesting that the old regulations be revised to avoid all measures that harm merchants and cause harassment.

Wine Industry Federation

The meeting was held at 1:00 PM. Over sixty representatives from various counties in Jiangsu Province attended. Wang Xiaolai, representing the City Chamber of Commerce, and Zhang Dalian, Huang Yuming, Chen Weiwen, Cheng Kefan, Xia Sunhuan, Xu Jianquan, and Chen Boying served as the presidium. The preparatory work was reported, followed by a speech by Wang Xiaolai, chairman of the City Chamber of Commerce, who briefly expressed his hope that the industry would unite, promote domestic goods, and prevent the invasion of foreign goods. Zhang Dalian, Chen Weiwen, Huang Yuming, Fang Zhongheng, Dai Zhuoan, Jin Jiayue, Chen Boying, Zhang Junren, Ding Jinsheng, Jin Yunjie, Gu Zhuyun, Liu Dezhi, Xia Sunhuan, Ming You'an, and Song Xingzui were elected as the fifteen executive committee members. Sun Jiannong, He Xiangsheng, Zhu Qingtang, Jin Juqing, Cheng Kefan, Gao Youming, and Zhu Runzhi were elected as the seven alternate committee members. Chen Fukang, Wang Baizhang, Wang Huanzhi, Shao Yuerun, Xie Zhendong, Xie Chuyu, and Qian Xiaoan were elected as the supervisory committee members, and Shen Weiya was the alternate. They immediately took the oath of office.

Central Telegrams

The representatives of the two industries telegraphed to Chairman Chiang and the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Industry, and Legislative Yuan yesterday, the text of which reads (abbreviated title): "Recently, we have learned that the General Taxation Department intends to change the 1933 tobacco and alcohol tax rates, abolish the public monopoly system, and replace it with a special tax on native tobacco leaves and a fixed tax on native alcohol, with a sudden increase in non-special tax amounts. Moreover, the tax collection starts from every 'jin' (a unit of weight), causing merchants to be harassed by trivial matters. The public monopoly system has been in place for a long time, and the people have been living in relative peace. If this sudden change is implemented, it will be no different from restoring the 'likin' system (internal transit tax). If it is implemented, it will not only increase the burden abruptly but also cause merchants to be blamed at every turn, possibly leading to the complete elimination of native tobacco and alcohol. This is tantamount to promoting foreign goods and destroying domestic products. Moreover, at a time when the commercial and rural economy is bankrupt, we are already struggling to save it. How can we bear to impose further harassment? Thinking about the future, we are extremely anxious. In addition to sending representatives with detailed information on the obstacles encountered in a separate letter, we are forwarding this telegram to request your kind consideration and approval to maintain the old system to reassure businesses and safeguard the livelihood of the people. We are extremely urgent. The United Representative Assembly of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Suzhou Tobacco and Alcohol Trade Associations kowtows."

Third Day of the Agricultural Products Exhibition in Shanghai County

Mrs. Niu Speaks Passionately About the Rural Economy

Yesterday (the 12th) was the third day of the Second Agricultural Products Exhibition in Shanghai County. It opened at 9:00 AM as scheduled. After judging, Mrs. Huang discussed ways to help the rural areas with Director Zhang for more than an hour. Mrs. Huang runs her own farm, farming and planting herself, which is truly rare in modern times. In this judging, each category was divided into three grades: A, B, and C. Products from government agencies were not judged. Grade A was for those that fully demonstrated excellent quality, Grade B was for those whose local appearance demonstrated excellent quality, and Grade C was for those that did not meet the above two standards. Inspection Reports of Two Banks

The 163rd Inspection Report of the Issue Reserve of the Central Bank states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issue of convertible banknotes of this bank. The 163rd inspection was held at the Issuing Bureau of this bank on June 10, 1933. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 44,788,620 silver dollars, including 40,424,357 silver dollar notes and 4,364,263 subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of convertible banknote reserves is 44,788,620 silver dollars, including 36,437,620 silver dollars in cash reserve. The cash reserve is kept in the issuing treasury of this bank (32,127,835 silver dollars), branches in various ports (2,527,170 silver dollars), and with other banks (1,782,615 silver dollars). The security reserve is equivalent to 8,351,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of Customs Gold Unit convertible banknotes issued is 417,269.40 Customs Gold Units. The total amount of Customs Gold Unit convertible banknote reserves is 417,269.40 Customs Gold Units. The reserve includes 7,004 taels and 6 qian and 9 fen of bullion, valued at 5957, equivalent to 417,269.40 Customs Gold Units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's convertible banknote regulations, 60% of the reserve should be in cash and 40% in security. The results of this inspection show that the cash exceeds 60% and the security is less than 40%. The ratio is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. June 10, 1933. Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun; Supervisors: Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiliang."

The 22nd Issue Reserve Report of the China Industrial Bank states: "The preparation of the issuing department of the China Industrial Bank has always been completely separated from the funds of the business department. The preparation is full. The number of issue preparations on June 10, 1933, is announced as follows: The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 25,138,661 yuan, including 16,114,661 yuan issued by this bank, 5,174,000 yuan issued by the United Bank, and 3,850,000 yuan used by various banks and Zhuang. In addition to the parts used by various banks and Zhuang, which are checked according to the original method, this inspection, the amount of convertible banknotes issued by the Union Bank is 21,128,861 yuan. The amount of convertible banknote reserves of the Union Bank is 21,128,861 yuan, including 12,812,661 yuan in cash reserve and 8,476,000 yuan in security reserve. The above two items, the gold reserve is more than 60% and the security reserve is less than 40%. All have been checked by Zhang Yiyan, an accountant from the Zhengze Accounting Firm, without error."

Special Publication

Shen Bao Series

Summary of the Soviet Union's Five-Year Agricultural Plan

Translated by Gao Zhi Full book 196 pages Paper cover 6-open format Actual price 50 cents

Although the content of the Soviet Union's five-year construction plan is a general social construction, it particularly focuses on agriculture, that is, the establishment of state labor farms and collective farms, and the industrialization of agriculture. Therefore, it is necessary for us to conduct a special study of the Soviet Union's five-year agricultural plan. This book is translated by Ms. Gao Zhixiang based on the English translation of the report and speech on agricultural construction plans by YAYakovlev, the Soviet Union's People's Commissar for Agriculture. The whole book is divided into five chapters. The first chapter first describes the large-scale agricultural organizations in the United States. Why should we talk about agriculture in the United States first? According to Yakolev: "A full understanding of the progress and current situation of agriculture in the Soviet Union cannot be obtained solely from research in the Soviet Union. In order to avoid errors in one's own evaluation of past results and future goals, it is necessary to begin comparing the new technological methods and large-scale developments in the Soviet Union and other capitalist countries, especially the United States. This comparison can clearly show the various characteristics of agricultural development in the Soviet Union, and it is also easy to analyze the advantages and disadvantages of our work." It can be seen that the importance of this chapter, really, from this comparative narrative, we can more clearly see how completely different the results obtained under two different economic systems are for the same event. The second chapter describes the large-scale agricultural organizations in the Soviet Union, explaining the rapid development of large-scale agriculture in the Soviet Union, the rapid increase of collective farms and state-owned farms, the gradual elimination of rich peasants, the gradual reduction of poor peasants, the full mechanization of agriculture, and the increasing socialization of the means of production; state-owned farms and collective farms have already achieved a substantial victory in the Soviet Union, which is not only empty talk, but has concrete facts to prove it. The third chapter describes the new tasks of agricultural development in the Soviet Union. These new tasks are for the first five-year plan, because the collectivization program in the first five-year plan was completed and exceeded in the spring of 1930, so the agricultural development plan must be fundamentally revised and its tasks re-determined. What are these new tasks? First, the consolidation of industrial agricultural products; second, the reconstruction of animal husbandry and the solution of the meat supply problem; third, the final solution of the grain production problem. This chapter describes these new tasks in five sections: animal husbandry, feed, grain consumption areas, wheat production areas, cotton, and flax. They are bravely advancing under the guidance of the party's general policy, based on the experience gained by the excellent vanguards and organizers of hundreds of thousands of large-scale farms, the collective farm members. "In the coming years, they will not only be able to completely solve the problem of food supply difficulties caused by low-productivity small-scale farms, but they believe that in a very short historical period, they will be able to meet the requirements of the Soviet Union's working masses at a rate of progress never known in capitalist society." The fourth chapter describes the organizational methods that the Soviet Union must have to consolidate and develop collective farms. In the Soviet Union, the rich peasants opposed the collective farms, and the middle peasants were wavering. How to make the general farmers participate in the collective farms and eliminate their reactionary forces is something that the Soviet Union is strictly planning. How they are planning is described in detail in this chapter. They firmly believe that no matter what difficulties stand in front of them, with the existing foundation of the Soviet Union, they will eventually be able to thoroughly achieve collectivization. Yakolev said: "We have these experiences behind us, and we stand on the basis of the party's general policy. We can boldly state that we must correct everything, no matter when, no matter who made the mistake. We will not allow anyone to hinder our collectivization from reaching its final goal, which is the creation of a socialist society!" The fifth chapter is a conclusion, which is a comprehensive explanation by Yakolev after the delegates discussed his report, and answers several questions. Finally, he said: "In short, our conclusion is based on the collectivization movement and state-owned farms. We can undoubtedly catch up with other countries more quickly than before." Indeed, looking at the past achievements of the Soviet Union's five-year agricultural plan, no one would say that his words are an exaggeration. Five appendices are attached at the end: 1. The Actual Record of Agricultural Collectivization in the First Five-Year Plan; 2. The Mechanization of Agriculture in the Soviet Union; 3. On Rural Work; 4. The Sorrow of American Farmers; 5. Collective Farm Movement and Agricultural Improvement. All are invaluable important reference materials, which can be mutually enlightening. At present, rural areas in all countries are suffering from extreme panic, especially in my country, where rural areas are under the oppression of foreign capitalism and are now completely bankrupt. Where exactly is the difference? It is really worth our study. The book can provide us with an important indication for this kind of research. Anyone who is concerned about Soviet agriculture and rural problems in my country must read this book. Eight illustrations are attached at the beginning.

Shen Bao Series

Essentials of Aviation in Europe and America

Compiled and written by Xu Yuanruo, the book has 76 pages, paperback, size 6 open, priced at 25 cents.

In modern warfare, due to the development of aviation, the air force has become a very important element. This book quotes the words of the British Spede, saying that the victory or defeat of future wars will not be determined by trenches or the sea, but by air combat. The importance of the air force in future wars is evident. As long as true world peace is not achieved, the great slaughter of mankind will be inevitable. The great power of the air force in future wars naturally deserves people's attention. Our country's existing naval and land forces are so poor and weak, not to mention the air force. However, the tempest of the times is approaching, and how can we be unprepared for a future world war? For a year, the Japanese air force has attacked our country in various places, and we should have tasted enough of this. What lessons has it given us? The purpose of this book is to introduce the general situation of the air forces of various countries and arouse the attention of the people to the air force. The whole book is divided into two chapters. The first chapter describes the current situation of the aviation circles of European and American powers, and is divided into two parts: military aviation and civil aviation. The United States, France, Britain, Italy, the Soviet Union, and other countries are described separately. From this, we can see how European and American countries, after being taught by the Great War, have drastically expanded their air forces and achieved amazing results in ten years. Not only has military aviation developed particularly, but civil aviation has also made rapid progress with government encouragement and private efforts. The development of civil aviation has an important meaning, that is, in wartime, these civil aviation aircraft can be immediately converted for military use. Therefore, strictly speaking, this kind of civil aviation can also be said to be a part of military aviation, and some countries attach more importance to civil aviation than military aviation, and the significance can be imagined. The second chapter describes the air defense of European and American powers. It is divided into four sections: 1) Air raids and losses of the powers in the European War, 2) European air defense before and during the war, 3) The current situation of air defense facilities of European and American powers, and 4) Civil air defense facilities of the powers. From this, we can know how particularly important a country's air defense equipment is, especially in wartime. If "a country is suffering from air raids by enemy planes, but it does not have its own planes to fight, then the country can immediately turn into ruins within a few hours." This does not need to be proven in books. The bombing of Zhabei by Japanese planes on January 28 is the best practical proof. This chapter describes the facts that European and American powers were threatened by enemy planes due to inadequate air defense equipment during the Great War and the current situation of air defense equipment. The whole book is very concise in describing the current situation of aviation in European and American powers, and it repeatedly emphasizes the importance of aviation. In fact, in today's world, "without an air force, there is no national defense," then how should the people feel after reading this?

(Nanjing, 12th) The Ministry of Education announced the regulations for school graduation certificates on the 12th. The main points are: 1) Students of all levels of schools who have completed their studies and passed their grades shall be given graduation certificates by the schools. In primary and secondary schools in places where graduation joint examinations are held, their graduation certificates shall be issued after passing the joint examination. 2) Colleges and above shall be stamped by the Ministry of Education, middle schools shall be stamped by the Department of Education or the administrative organ of the directly subordinate municipalities, and elementary schools shall be stamped by the municipal or county educational administrative organ directly subordinate to the administrative organ.

Fujian Department of Education Rectification

Steps and Plans for Vocational Education

(Fuzhou Correspondent) Zheng Zhenwen, Director of the Fujian Department of Education, believes that vocational education is extremely important and should be sorted out and the steps and implementation plans should be determined. The following is a reference:

There are a total of sixteen vocational schools in this province, public and private. Six of them belong to the province: Fuzhou Vocational Middle School, Fuzhou Polytechnic Middle School, Fuzhou Agricultural and Forestry Middle School, Longxi Vocational Middle School, Nanping Vocational Middle School, and Xiamen Vocational Middle School. Five of them belong to the county: Minhou Vocational Middle School, Minhou No. 1 Girls' Vocational Middle School, Minhou No. 2 Girls' Vocational Middle School, Nan'an Vocational School, and Minqing Xidong Girls' Middle School. Five of them are private: Jimei Commercial School, Jimei Agricultural and Forestry School, Jimei Fisheries and Navigation School, Rantian Vocational Middle School, and Siming Minnan Vocational Middle School.

In the future, funds will be raised and equipment will be expanded. The funds for vocational schools in the province will be allocated from the provincial education funds. The funds for vocational schools in the county will be allocated from the county education funds. The funds for private schools will be allocated from donations from the school board, or from the interest of the school fund and the collection of tuition fees. In the future, the province plans to increase the funding year by year so that the funds for vocational schools account for 5% to 25% of the provincial education funds. At the same time, it plans to cooperate with the provincial construction and construction committee and various industrial groups to invest and cooperate in holding various production-oriented vocational training. The county and private schools are also instructed to raise funds to enrich the equipment, or find ways to sell their products, which can be used for considerable subsidies.

The steps for adding schools are based on the principle of whether education funds can be increased year by year. Judging from the current situation of various vocational schools, the number of secondary vocational schools is actually the majority. In the future, while focusing on the promotion of ordinary vocational training, the vocational training classes of various vocational schools will be expanded to achieve the popularization of vocational education. At the same time, it is planned to add specialized vocational schools to provide further education for vocational school students and reserve teachers for advanced vocational schools. Therefore, it is decided to plan to add an agricultural and forestry specialty school starting in the 22nd year, so that it can be more profound and practical. Starting in the 24th year, it is planned to add a medical specialty school to prepare for the province's medical talent reserve. Starting in the 26th year, it is planned to add an industrial specialty school to meet the needs of the province's industry.

The plan to reorganize the original vocational schools 1) Avoid duplication of courses. Vocational schools in the same area with the same courses will be ordered to merge or change to other courses that meet the needs. 2) Reorganize the establishment of various schools. The junior high school classes that also handle ordinary courses in vocational schools will be ordered to stop or transfer to the middle school for management. All vocational schools will open up vocational classes. 3) Enrich the number of students. While defining the methods for vocational schools to collect various fees, a method for subsidizing students' work and labor achievements will be formulated. 4) Open up student employment opportunities. Within the 22nd year, the purpose of setting up departments in various schools will be specially defined. Vocational skills that are used for appreciation or leisure classes will be gradually enrolled, and talents needed in local agricultural production and manufacturing or in the province's construction plan will be given priority to training. In the future, when short-term primary school children are employed, vocational schools will hold various apprentice classes, and the teachers will be vocational school graduates. It is also planned to jointly set up a general sales office for the products of various schools in the provincial capital or larger cities in the province, and attach a vocational guidance center to promote the guidance of local industries and the introduction of graduates.

Students from this city participating in the joint examination

Can Get Group Discount for Taking the Bus

Those who cannot participate due to special reasons must report one day in advance

The joint graduation examination for primary and secondary schools in this city has been decided to be held on the 15th of this month. The Municipal Bureau of Education, in view of the fact that the participating schools are on the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou, and Songhu railway lines, has specifically verified the established cases in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. Students can get a discount for taking the bus back and forth according to the group bus fare regulations. A notice has been issued yesterday, and the schools can directly contact the railway bureau to handle the matter. In addition, if students participating in the joint examination cannot participate in the joint examination due to illness or special circumstances, the schools shall submit a report to the Bureau of Education for a make-up examination. The procedures for approving this report should be submitted to the Bureau of Education one day before the joint examination, together with supporting documents, for verification.

Municipal Education Association

Held an Extraordinary Board Meeting Yesterday

Submit a Report to the Ministry of Education Allowing Students with Two Failed Subjects in the Joint Examination to Provisionally Advance

The Summer Academic Seminar is Scheduled to Start on July 3

The Shanghai Municipal Education Association held its third extraordinary board meeting at 3 pm yesterday. Those present were Zheng Hongnian, Huang Zaoxiong, Wu Xiu, Chen Jicheng, Ma Jiazhen, Xu Zeyu, and Tao Bai. Zhou Darong and Mao Yun were present. The chairman was Huang Zaoxiong, and the recorder was Zhang Lichun. The proceedings were as usual. Matters for discussion: 1) Requesting review of the Shanghai Municipal Education Association's rules for the appointment, dismissal, and service of staff in public schools. It was resolved to amend and pass it. 2) The graduation joint examination regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Education stipulate that students who fail one or two subjects in the joint examination shall not be allowed to advance and must pass the next joint examination before they can advance. Then the students will be wasting time and losing their studies before participating in the next joint examination. Should the Ministry of Education be requested to make a supplementary case? It was resolved to request the Bureau of Education to telegraph the Ministry of Education. Due to the imminent examination period, the Association will telegraph the Ministry of Education separately. Except for the three subjects of Chinese, English, and Mathematics, students who fail one or two subjects in the joint examination shall be allowed to provisionally advance as special students and can only be changed to formal students after passing the make-up examination in the next joint examination and obtaining a diploma.

3) How should the Association's summer academic seminar be conducted? It was resolved that (A) the period should be set for five weeks, starting on July 3rd; (B) the location should be set at the Municipal Shuji Primary School in the Tianhou Temple in the Public Concession; (C) the following courses should be offered: 1) Philosophy of Life, 2) Technical Politics, 3) International Politics, 4) History of Chinese Economic Thought, 5) Constitution, 6) General Outline of Current Chinese Law, 7) Practical English Rhetoric, 8) English Phonetics, 9) General Outline of Sinology, 10) Fine Arts Lecture, 11) Mandarin Phonetics and Grammar, 12) Educational Testing and Statistics, 13) Practical Common Sense of Drug Medicine, 14) Chemical Problems, 15) Physical Problems, 16) Algebra, Geometry, Trigonometry, Analytical Geometry; (D) It is presumed that Director Zheng Hongnian will be the chairman, Director Tao Baichuan will be the vice-chairman, and Director Wu Xiu will be the secretary-general; (E) The lecturers for each course will be hired by the chairman from professors in various universities and authorities in academic circles; (F) The fee for selecting each course is two yuan, and at least two courses must be selected. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Jinan University Enrolls New Students for the Next Semester

Enrollment Quotas and Dates Are Confirmed

National Jinan University is the only highest institution for cultivating overseas Chinese youths. After the war, President Zheng actively improved it and restored its old appearance. Recently, he spent half a year rigorously reviewing the articles of association in order to meet the actual needs and emphasize the education of science and production. The newly revised curriculum has been compiled and will be implemented starting in the 22nd year. In recent years, in order to facilitate the enrollment of overseas Chinese children, the enrollment dates are later than other schools. Now, in order to improve the enrollment level of new students, this year's enrollment will be held in July. The registration and guarantee dates are set from July 23rd to 25th, and the examination dates are set from July 28th to 29th. As for overseas Chinese students, in addition to notifying overseas Chinese schools in various places to inform returning overseas Chinese students that they must come to the school early to take the examination, they will still be given preferential treatment, that is, the registration date will be extended from August 2nd to 5th, and the examination dates will be changed to August 7th to 8th. The law and education colleges of the school were abolished last summer by order of the Ministry. Now President Zheng is actively expanding the three colleges of liberal arts, science, and commerce, and is especially committed to the various facilities of the science and commerce colleges. This year, in addition to enrolling freshmen in the three colleges of liberal arts, science, and commerce, only second-year students in various departments of the science college are enrolled. Transfer students in other colleges and departments are not enrolled. As for the middle school department, because it only enrolls overseas Chinese students and does not enroll mainland students, the enrollment date remains the same, that is, registration starts from August 15th to 20th, and the examination is on August 24th to 25th. This year, it is planned to enroll 40 freshmen in the first year of junior high school, 40 freshmen in the general high school, 40 freshmen in the teacher training high school, 18 transfer students in the second year of junior high school, and 12 transfer students in the second year of high school. To know the details of the school's enrollment, a prospectus is available, and a two-cent stamp is attached for mailing.

Sports

Issue of Venue Reclamation by the Athletic Association

Talks with Shen Siliang

The Association Has Not Yet Received Formal Notification

Even if Reclaimed, It Won't Cause Problems for the Association

For Shanghai's Sake, a Sports Field Should Be Found

The matter of the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation's venue on Route Pére Robert in this city being reclaimed by the landowner, the Rockefeller Foundation, and donated to the National Medical College has drawn much attention from the sports community. Yesterday, the reporter visited Shen Siliang, the honorary director of the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation, to inquire about the truth of the venue situation and future plans. A detailed record is provided below.

No Notification Yet

The Rockefeller Foundation Wants to Reclaim the Venue

And Donate it to the National Medical College

The matter has already been seen in the newspapers, but the Athletic Federation has not yet received a formal notification. As for the construction of the hospital, this is a major undertaking and cannot be accomplished in a short period of time. Therefore, even if the venue is reclaimed, it can still be temporarily borrowed. There should be no problem for this winter's soccer season.

History of Venue Reclamation

The soccer field, track and field, basketball court,

And tennis court were initially managed by Gray (the sports director of the National YMCA), the Chinese Commissioner and Director-General of the Far Eastern Games, with the remaining funds from the fifth Far Eastern Games. The baseball field was operated privately by Grew and Biers, incurring a loss of over ten thousand yuan. When the Athletic Federation took it back, it received assistance from Cheng Yize. Therefore, Cheng's contribution was significant in the recovery of the baseball field. The several acres of vacant land behind the soccer field had long been sold to the French Municipal Council by the Rockefeller Foundation, and the Huatong Public School has now been built and opened.

Tennis Stars and Tennis Flower

The Newlyweds Lin Liang Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday

Staying at the Cangzhou Hotel, a Banquet for Friends and Relatives Last Night

Scheduled to Depart for Sichuan on a Honeymoon Trip on the 26th

Tennis national player Mr. Lin Huajun and tennis flower Ms. Liang Peiyu held their wedding on Saturday, the 10th of this month, in Tianjin. The union of these heroes and beauties is a wonderful story in the history of Chinese sports. The newlyweds Lin and Liang arrived in Shanghai from Tianjin yesterday afternoon and were warmly welcomed by friends and relatives. The newlyweds are staying at the Cangzhou Hotel and plan to travel to Sichuan for their honeymoon on the 26th of this month.

From Love to Marriage Ms. Liang, accompanied by her sister Ms. Peiyao, represented Tianjin at the National Games in Hangzhou in the spring of the 19th year, winning a championship and gaining fame throughout the country. After returning to Shanghai from Hangzhou, she stayed briefly in Shanghai due to illness, where she met Mr. Lin. From then on, their relationship blossomed on the tennis court and grew stronger over time, leading to their engagement. However, it was never announced until three weeks ago when they officially announced their engagement in Tianjin. Due to the current situation, they advanced the wedding date. The British Consulate Served as the Witness The wedding ceremony was held at the British Consulate in Tianjin at 11 AM on Saturday, witnessed by the British Consul in Tianjin. Chinese and foreign guests were present, making it a grand occasion. Ms. Liang's father, Liang Yanqing, is a prominent Cantonese merchant in Tianjin, and her brother is a compradore at Jardine Matheson, with extensive social connections.

Honeymooning in Sichuan After the wedding, they took a fast train south that evening, arriving at the Shanghai North Railway Station at 5 PM yesterday, and went to the Cangzhou Hotel to rest. Last night, friends and relatives in Shanghai hosted a banquet to congratulate them. The newlyweds will travel to Sichuan for their honeymoon on the 26th of this month. The newlyweds' exploration of Sichuan will be exciting, but it is feared that Mr. Lin's skills will not be seen on the tennis court this season. (Photo by Wang Kaifu)

The Association's Strength Is Insufficient

The association has already

Exerted a lot of competitive force on this venue

Initially, it made several requests to the Rockefeller Foundation to donate the land, but ultimately it was unsuccessful. This was because there were many people who wanted the land, and many of them were from the medical field. The Rockefeller Foundation also focused on medical endeavors, so the medical community's requests had a greater effect. This is why the National Medical College was successful. Another factor is that the land tax of the French Municipal Council has increased sharply in recent years. Initially, the entire land only required two hundred taels per month, but now it requires two thousand taels, an increase of tenfold. Therefore, even if the land is not reclaimed, the association would not have the financial resources to pay the land tax.

It's Not a Problem for the Association

After the land is reclaimed, there will be no

problems on the association's side. The association is a national amateur sports administrative organization, and it only needs to establish an office. There is no need for the establishment of a sports field. However, for the sake of the entire Shanghai sports community, a sports field must be found. The association's board of directors and enthusiastic sports supporters have contacted various parties several times.

Difficulty in Finding a Venue

The Shanghai sports community will be greatly affected after the venue is reclaimed. Therefore, a suitable location must be found to develop a sports field. Yangshupu, Xujiahui, and the Jiangwan city center have all been inspected. The land is sufficient for use, but it is either too expensive or the transportation is inconvenient, making them unsuitable. Now, they are looking in the western part of Shanghai (not on Route de Sikawei). Although the location is slightly remote, the transportation is relatively convenient. Among unsatisfactory options, it is relatively suitable. Therefore, the goal for the venue is generally to focus on the western part of Shanghai. Previously, the association favored the former Shanghai Greyhound Racing Stadium, but the land price was too high and could not become a reality.

The Association's Fundraising Issues

As for how the association will manage its finances, this is also not a problem. The equipment on the field is no longer valuable. The writing room and basketball room cannot be dismantled because the contract stipulated that any fixed buildings on the field could not be dismantled when the land was reclaimed. Therefore, the association has always been hesitant to invest in construction, fearing that the money would be wasted if the land was reclaimed.

Future Sports Situation

Because of this proposed reclamation of the association's land, enthusiastic sports supporters in Shanghai are considering forming a Shanghai Amateur Sports Association to govern the competitive sports in Shanghai. The association greatly hopes this can be realized. In this way, the association would not need to oversee Shanghai's sports affairs and could fully focus on national sports affairs and the promotion of international sports.

A Sports Field Can Be Found in the Xietu Road Area

An Opinion from an Enthusiastic Sports Supporter

Shen expressed his opinion on the issue of finding a venue, as mentioned above. Now, an enthusiastic sports supporter says that the reason why the baseball field has flourished to this day is that it is close to Ximen, surrounded by schools, densely populated, and has convenient transportation. Therefore, when looking for a venue, it should be in an area with a large population, such as the Xietu Road area. There is a lot of vacant land, the transportation is convenient, and it is not far from Route Pére Robert, making it very suitable.

Chinese Wrestling Association Welcomes Chairman

The Chinese Wrestling Association was organized by Chen Fengming, Yang Xiaowen, Hu Zhuoru, Zhu Wenwei, Zhang Huichuan, Wang Huaiting, and other disciples of the famous martial artist Tong Zhongyi. The association is located at No. 23, Lane 124, Tongfu Road, at the intersection of Weihaiwei Road, and its purpose is to promote the national art of wrestling. In order to develop its affairs, the association has hired Tong as the chairman and Fan Chongshi, Liu Xiang's representative in Shanghai, as the vice chairman. Tong is currently the director of the Shaolin branch of the Shanghai Municipal Guoshu (National Martial Arts) Hall and is also proficient in wrestling, making him a famous martial artist in our country. Fan has always loved martial arts and also has a deep understanding of wrestling. The association is fortunate to have these two gentlemen serve as chairman and vice chairman. It is reported that a banquet was held at the Zhimelou Restaurant at 7 PM last night to welcome the chairman and vice chairman.

Random Thoughts

Lin Pengxia and Shi Tiansun

— Zhan Kang

China's first female pilot, Ms. Lin Pengxia, came alone from the provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, Ningxia, Suiyuan, and Chahar, talking extensively about her experiences returning from the Northwest. For a time, people in academic circles highly praised her, calling her China's amazing woman. When I read this in the newspaper, I felt both joy and sadness about the phrase "China's first female pilot." I was happy that there was a woman like Ms. Lin who, with a spirit of great fearlessness, was opening a new era for female pilots. I was sad that in this world where air forces are increasing year after year, China has long claimed to have female pilots, but why is it that only today do we have this "China's first female pilot" Ms. Lin Pengxia?

Back in the yearnings of sixteen years ago, when the European War had not yet ended, the American pilot Ms. Shi Tiansun came to Jiangwan, Shanghai, to demonstrate flying an airplane, receiving a grand welcome from the people of Shanghai. If the women of our country had all worked hard together at that time, would we have had to wait for Ms. Lin to be the trailblazer after such a long period of sixteen years? Female pilots would have emerged one after another long ago. Sixteen years ago, I jokingly drafted a "Message Welcoming Female Pilot Shi Tiansun on Behalf of the Female Community," At that time, humorous articles focused on parallelism and antithesis, and the original text is as follows:

"With lofty ambitions reaching the clouds, and a heart longing to chase lightning; she is not Chang'e, the goddess who flies to the moon, but like a heavenly maiden scattering flowers. Transcending the mundane, she is filled with admiration for the beauty of the West, flying in the clouds, she actually becomes a true person in the sky. Standing behind a screen, walking on a perfuming burner, is not enough to describe her agility; magpies forming a bridge, Qingdao as an envoy, have already yielded to her supernatural powers. Coming down from the sky, Sima Guang's analogy of taking a high official's cap is just empty words; riding the wind in the cold, Lie Yukou's fable actually becomes reality." "Excerpted" We, who are confined to the boudoir, yearn for the blue sky; even if we have the telepathic heart of a rhinoceros horn, we regret not having the wings of a pair of colorful phoenixes; since we are not willing to remain submissive, we are bound to strive to fly high. Those who soar three thousand miles high, the pilots who are high above, can be said to be very far away; those who knock on the eight or nine layers of heaven, we, the mediocre and incapable sisters, do not know how to encourage ourselves?

The final couplet was to encourage the general female community, teaching them to rise up in response and become comparable to Shi Tiansun, but only Lin Pengxia has done so. My fictitious welcoming text can of course be transferred to Ms. Lin. However, after this long period of time, the possibility of transferring it to China's first female pilot has only now arisen, something I never dreamed of when I wrote it back then.

Cholera Comes to Market

— Yongzi

After the loquats turn yellow, the green plums also ripen. The weather gets hotter day by day, and then "cholera" comes to market. "Cholera" does not seek to improve itself. The more high-class the family, the more "cholera" keeps its distance. The more "common" people become, the worse things get, and as they become "poor," "cholera" becomes more intimate with them.

Brother Fly is "cholera's" "volunteer travel agency." Through the power of the "volunteer travel agency," he roams between "weird, weird, ten coppers a cup" of "Dutch-made Holland water," "sweet honey, ten coppers a slice" of watermelon, "white sugar London cake," and "cool chestnut cake." Cold noodle stalls, sour plum soup, and all kinds of sour, spoiled, and rotten "delicacies" are all "cholera's" "summer retreats," for everything that Brother Fly relies upon to live. Common people and poor people, ambitious, swallow cholera's "summer resorts" in one gulp, clearly "pulling the tiger's whiskers," "offending the tiger's might," "stirring up trouble on the god of the year," "cholera" will not give up and will rummage around in your stomach like Sun Wukong, pulling your collar and dragging you to King Yama's court to file a lawsuit.

Of course, the best way to avoid being disturbed by "cholera" is to stay away from its "summer resorts," and on the other hand, get a "vaccination" first to implement "internal security." If you are not careful and "cholera" has already attacked your "hinterland," then you should quickly retreat to the epidemic hospital for "long-term resistance" and never be tough, lest you become "cholera's" captive. Some people like to ask barbers to scrape sha, which is like using a breech-loading gun to resist a machine gun, and "cholera" will laugh so hard it howls.

"Cholera" has come to market, everyone must be careful of fire, and issue a curfew order. Get a "vaccination" to implement "internal security" to prevent "internal reaction." At the same time, when dealing with "imported goods," you must carefully consider and check them before passing them. If Brother Fly arrives uninvited, issue an eviction order, or even take "decisive action," which is the fundamental way to "ban cholera." Please, citizens, "unite spiritually" and "defeat cholera!"
